<p><b>Karim Mostafa Benzema</b> (<small>French pronunciation:&#160;&#8203;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/French" title="Help:IPA/French">[kaim mstafa bnzema]</a></span>; born 19 December 1987) is a French professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a> for Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a>. Known for his aerial ability, workrate, playmaking and finishing, Benzema is considered to be one of the best strikers in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-Bio_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bio-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Lyon" title="Lyon">Lyon</a>, Benzema began his senior career with hometown club <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Olympique Lyonnais</a> in 2005, contributing sporadically to three <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> title wins. In <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Ligue_1" title="2007–08 Ligue 1">2008</a>, he was named the <a href="/wiki/National_Union_of_Professional_Footballers" title="National Union of Professional Footballers">National Union of Professional Footballers</a> (UNFP) <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Player of the Year</a> and in the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#2008" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Team of the Year</a> as he finished as the league's <a href="/wiki/Top_goalscorers_in_Ligue_1" class="mw-redirect" title="Top goalscorers in Ligue 1">top goalscorer</a> and won his fourth title and first <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a>. In 2009, Benzema was the subject of a then French record <a href="/wiki/Most_expensive_association_football_transfer" class="mw-redirect" title="Most expensive association football transfer">association football transfer</a> when signed for Real Madrid in a <a href="/wiki/Transfer_(association_football)" title="Transfer (association football)">transfer</a> worth €35&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After struggling to establish himself in his debut season, Benzema eventually reached prominence at Real Madrid and has won 13 trophies, including three <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> titles, two <a href="/wiki/Copas_del_Rey" class="mw-redirect" title="Copas del Rey">Copas del Rey</a>, and four <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> titles, and ranks as the club's fifth <a href="/wiki/List_of_Real_Madrid_CF_records_and_statistics#Goalscorers" title="List of Real Madrid CF records and statistics">all-time top goalscorer</a>, as well as their all-time top assist provider.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> While at Real Madrid, Benzema has also been named <a href="/wiki/France_Football#French_Player_of_the_Year" title="France Football">French Player of the Year</a> three times.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">French</a> international, Benzema won the <a href="/wiki/2004_UEFA_European_Under-17_Championship" title="2004 UEFA European Under-17 Championship">2004 UEFA European Under-17 Championship</a> and made his senior debut for France in 2007, at age 19. He has since earned over 80 caps, including appearing and scoring in three major tournaments: the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">2008</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">2012</a> editions of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship" title="UEFA European Championship">UEFA European Championship</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>. He scored his first goal in a <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game" title="Exhibition game">friendly</a> against <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austria</a>, and ranks as his nation's tenth <a href="/wiki/List_of_leading_goalscorers_for_the_France_national_football_team" title="List of leading goalscorers for the France national football team">all-time top goalscorer</a>. Benzema was controversially left out of the squad for the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 World Cup</a>, and has not played for France after being implicated in a publicised scandal involving blackmail in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:27%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"When I was younger, the way <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a> played had an influence on me. For me, he's the best striker of all-time. I watch videos of him, and try to do what he does, but it's not easy. It's impossible to pull off the same moves as he did."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—Benzema on the influence of his idol, Brazilian striker Ronaldo, on his own career.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Benzema began his football career at his hometown club Bron Terraillon SC at the age of eight. While at the club, he was nicknamed <i>Coco</i> by friends and, after scoring two goals in an under-10 match against the <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais_Reserves_and_Academy" title="Olympique Lyonnais Reserves and Academy">Lyon youth academy</a>, began attracting attention from the biggest club in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-benzema_class_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_class-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> According to Serge Santa Cruz, who was president of Bron Terraillon in the 1990s, Lyon officials had visited him directly in an attempt to sign the youngster; however, Santa Cruz refused.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_youth_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_youth-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> After talking with Benzema's father, the club allowed the player to undergo a trial with Lyon.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_youth_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_youth-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Following the trial, Benzema officially joined Lyon and was inserted into the club's academy.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lyon">Lyon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Lyon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Benzema quickly ascended up the youth categories in the academy. He served as a <a href="/wiki/Ballboy" class="mw-redirect" title="Ballboy">ballboy</a> during Lyon senior team matches and performed well in school being described as a student who was "discreet and respectful".<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_youth_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_youth-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> At under-16 level, Benzema scored 38 goals in the <i>Championnat National des 16 ans</i>, the domestic league for under-16 youth players in France.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_Ligue_1" title="2004–05 Ligue 1">2004–05 season</a>, Benzema was promoted to the club's reserve team, which was playing in the <a href="/wiki/Championnat_de_France_amateur" class="mw-redirect" title="Championnat de France amateur">Championnat de France amateur</a>, the fourth division of <a href="/wiki/Football_in_France" title="Football in France">French football</a>. Despite only playing with the team during the autumn campaign, he scored a team-high ten goals as the Lyon reserve team finished second in its group.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2004.E2.80.9307:_Breakthrough_and_three_league_titles"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2004–07:_Breakthrough_and_three_league_titles">2004–07: Breakthrough and three league titles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 2004–07: Breakthrough and three league titles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Benzema was called up to the senior team for the first time under manager <a href="/wiki/Paul_Le_Guen" title="Paul Le Guen">Paul Le Guen</a> during the break leading up to the second half of the season. As is customary with new players arriving at Lyon, the young striker had to stand up and speak to his new teammates, which at that time included the likes of <a href="/wiki/Michael_Essien" title="Michael Essien">Michael Essien</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sylvain_Wiltord" title="Sylvain Wiltord">Sylvain Wiltord</a>, <a href="/wiki/Florent_Malouda" title="Florent Malouda">Florent Malouda</a> and <a href="/wiki/Eric_Abidal" title="Eric Abidal">Eric Abidal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_fifa_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_fifa-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> While speaking, Benzema was subjected to jokes and laughter, which prompted the youngster to declare, "Do not laugh, I'm here to take your place."<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_fifa_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_fifa-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> He, subsequently, made his professional debut on 15 January 2005 against <a href="/wiki/FC_Metz" title="FC Metz">Metz</a>, appearing as a substitute for <a href="/wiki/Pierre-Alain_Frau" title="Pierre-Alain Frau">Pierre-Alain Frau</a>. Lyon won the match 2–0 as Benzema provided the assist on the second goal scored by <a href="/wiki/Bryan_Bergougnoux" title="Bryan Bergougnoux">Bryan Bergougnoux</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_class_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_class-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> He would subsequently sign his first professional contract, agreeing to a three-year deal.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> After making three more appearances as a substitute, on 2 April Benzema made his first professional start in a 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">Lens</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> He finished the campaign with six appearances as Lyon won its fourth-straight league title.
</p><p>Benzema began the <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_Ligue_1" title="2005–06 Ligue 1">2005–06 season</a> under the tutelage of new manager <a href="/wiki/G%C3%A9rard_Houllier" title="Gérard Houllier">Gérard Houllier</a>. Under Houllier, he struggled for meaningful minutes due to the presence of newly signed Brazilian striker <a href="/wiki/Fred_(footballer,_born_1983)" title="Fred (footballer, born 1983)">Fred</a>, as well as Sylvain Wiltord. Benzema made his season debut on 2 October 2005 in a league win over <a href="/wiki/Stade_Rennais_F.C." title="Stade Rennais F.C.">Rennes</a>, appearing as a substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On 6 December, he made his <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> debut in Lyon's final group stage match against <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norwegian</a> club <a href="/wiki/Rosenborg_BK" title="Rosenborg BK">Rosenborg</a>. On his competition debut, he scored his first professional goal in a 2–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> A month later, Benzema scored his first professional double in a 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Grenoble_Foot_38" title="Grenoble Foot 38">Grenoble</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> On 4 March 2006, Benzema scored his first professional league goal against <a href="/wiki/AC_Ajaccio" title="AC Ajaccio">Ajaccio</a> in a 3–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema began earning more playing time in the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_Ligue_1" title="2006–07 Ligue 1">2006–07 season</a> and made his competitive season debut in the <a href="/wiki/2006_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2006 Trophée des Champions">2006 Trophée des Champions</a> against <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a>. In the French Supercup, Benzema converted a penalty which drew the match at 1–1. Lyon later won the league curtain-raiser 5–4 on penalties.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Benzema opened the league campaign on a quick note scoring in the team's first match of the season against <a href="/wiki/FC_Nantes" title="FC Nantes">Nantes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Three weeks later, on 26 August 2006, Benzema appeared as a substitute and scored two goals in a 4–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/OGC_Nice" title="OGC Nice">Nice</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He also converted two goals in the Champions League group stage against <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romanian</a> outfit <a href="/wiki/FC_Steaua_Bucure%C8%99ti" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Steaua Bucureti">Steaua Bucureti</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> club <a href="/wiki/FC_Dynamo_Kyiv" title="FC Dynamo Kyiv">Dynamo Kyiv</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> After appearing regularly during the autumn campaign, on 10 November, Benzema suffered a severe thigh injury.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> The injury resulted in the striker missing three months of action before returning in February 2007. Benzema failed to score a goal until the final league match of the season against Nantes as Lyon recorded its sixth consecutive league title.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2007.E2.80.9309:_Club_talisman"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2007–09:_Club_talisman">2007–09: Club talisman</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2007–09: Club talisman">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>For the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Ligue_1" title="2007–08 Ligue 1">2007–08 season</a>, with Florent Malouda, <a href="/wiki/John_Carew" title="John Carew">John Carew</a> and Sylvain Wiltord all departing from the club, Benzema switched to the number 10 shirt and was inserted into the lead striker role. After forming a special relationship with new manager <a href="/wiki/Alain_Perrin" title="Alain Perrin">Alain Perrin</a>, he responded with 31 goals in 51 games. He topped the league with 20 goals, scored four goals in the Champions League, one in the <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="Coupe de la Ligue">Coupe de la Ligue</a> and totaled six goals in six Coupe de France matches, helping Lyon win their first ever <a href="/wiki/Double_(association_football)" title="Double (association football)">double</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Some of his more dazzling performances that season included a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> against Metz on 15 September,<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> an <a href="/wiki/Equaliser_(sports)" title="Equaliser (sports)">equalizing goal</a> in the 90th minute from a <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">free kick</a> against <a href="/wiki/Derby_du_Rh%C3%B4ne" class="mw-redirect" title="Derby du Rhône">Derby du Rhône</a> rivals <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> and a goal against Lens that was nominated for goal of the season by fans.
</p><p>In the Champions League, Benzema scored an important double against <a href="/wiki/Rangers_F.C." title="Rangers F.C.">Rangers</a> at <a href="/wiki/Ibrox_Stadium" title="Ibrox Stadium">Ibrox Stadium</a> on the last match day of the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_UEFA_Champions_League#Group_stage" title="2007–08 UEFA Champions League">group stage</a>. The 3–0 victory assured Lyon progression to the knockout rounds.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League_2007%E2%80%9308#Knockout_stage" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA Champions League 2007–08">knockout rounds</a>, Lyon faced <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> and Benzema continued to score, this time it was from outside the <a href="/wiki/Penalty_area" title="Penalty area">penalty box</a> in the first leg match which ended in a 1–1 draw<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> and United eventually won the tie 1–2 on aggregate. Manchester United manager <a href="/wiki/Alex_Ferguson" title="Alex Ferguson">Sir Alex Ferguson</a> and players praised Benzema for his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Lyon club president <a href="/wiki/Jean-Michel_Aulas" title="Jean-Michel Aulas">Jean-Michel Aulas</a> later accused Ferguson of <a href="/wiki/Tapping-up" class="mw-redirect" title="Tapping-up">tapping-up</a> Benzema.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:30%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"It's a compliment to be compared to <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>, but we are different players."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><small>—Benzema in 2008 after being compared to his French compatriot Zidane.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> </small></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 13 March 2008, Benzema extended his contract with Lyon until 2013 with a one-year extension option.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> After signing his new contract, Benzema became one of the highest paid footballers in France.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> For his efforts that season, he was named the Ligue 1 <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Player of the Year</a>, selected to the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#2009" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Team of the Year</a> and awarded the Trophée du Meilleur Buteur for being the league's top scorer.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> He won the <a href="/wiki/Bravo_Award" title="Bravo Award">2008 Bravo Award</a> given to the most outstanding young footballer playing in Europe,<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> and was also shortlisted by French magazine <i><a href="/wiki/France_Football" title="France Football">France Football</a></i> for the <a href="/wiki/2008_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2008 Ballon d&#39;Or">2008 Ballon d'Or</a> award,<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> eventually won by <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>.
</p><p>Benzema got off to a good start for the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Ligue_1" title="2008–09 Ligue 1">2008–09 season</a>, scoring twice in Lyon's opening league match against <a href="/wiki/Toulouse_FC" title="Toulouse FC">Toulouse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> The following three weeks, he scored goals against <a href="/wiki/Rh%C3%B4ne-Alpes" title="Rhône-Alpes">Rhône-Alpes</a> rivals <a href="/wiki/Grenoble_Foot_38" title="Grenoble Foot 38">Grenoble</a><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> and Saint-Étienne<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> and scored a goal against Nice, converting a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a> in the dying seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Lyon won all three matches. As a result of his early goals, Lyon club president Jean-Michel Aulas quelled the many transfer rumors surrounding Benzema by placing a €100&#160;million price tag on the striker. He was also nominated alongside <a href="/wiki/Franck_Rib%C3%A9ry" title="Franck Ribéry">Franck Ribéry</a> to be featured on the French cover of the video game <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_09" title="FIFA 09">FIFA 09</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Karim_Benzema_17586.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Karim_Benzema_17586.jpg/200px-Karim_Benzema_17586.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Karim_Benzema_17586.jpg/300px-Karim_Benzema_17586.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Karim_Benzema_17586.jpg/400px-Karim_Benzema_17586.jpg 2x" data-file-width="520" data-file-height="390" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Karim_Benzema_17586.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema during a training session with Lyon</div></div></div>
<p>He scored his seventh goal of the league on 29 October, scoring in the 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Sochaux-Montb%C3%A9liard" title="FC Sochaux-Montbéliard">Sochaux</a>. Benzema scored again the following weekend in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Le_Mans_FC" title="Le Mans FC">Le Mans</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> He was among the top scorers in the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2008–09 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> group stage, scoring five goals,<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> a double against Steaua Bucureti,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> two goals in two matches against <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> and a goal against the eventual group winners <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> on the final match day.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the <a href="/wiki/Christmas_and_holiday_season" title="Christmas and holiday season">winter break</a>, Benzema endured a rough patch going scoreless the first three games before recording his 11th goal of the season against Nice in a 3–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Two weeks later, he scored his 12th goal against <a href="/wiki/AS_Nancy" title="AS Nancy">Nancy</a> in a 2–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> The next nine matches, both Benzema and Lyon's form dwindled losing four matches, drawing three and winning only two with Benzema scoring only two goals in that stretch, both of them against Le Mans in a 3–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> The bad form resulted in Lyon losing their grip on first-place position and eventually falling out of the title race, thus ending their streak of seven consecutive Ligue 1 titles.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Benzema was a part of four of those title runs.
</p><p>Despite losing the title, Benzema got back on track scoring his 15th and 16th goals of the season on 17 May in a 3–1 away victory over rivals <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a>, the first goal being a penalty.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> He scored his 17th goal the following weekend against <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">Caen</a> in a 3–1 victory moving him into third place among Ligue 1 top scorers.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Madrid">Real Madrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Real Madrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2009.E2.80.9310:_Transfer_and_adapting_to_Spain"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2009–10:_Transfer_and_adapting_to_Spain">2009–10: Transfer and adapting to Spain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2009–10: Transfer and adapting to Spain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 1 July 2009, it was announced that Lyon had reached an agreement with Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> for the transfer of Benzema. The transfer fee was priced at €35&#160;million with the fee rising to as much as €41&#160;million based on incentives.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> On 9 July, Benzema successfully passed his medical and signed his contract, a six-year deal, later that afternoon.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> He was presented officially as a Real Madrid player later that night at the <a href="/wiki/Santiago_Bernab%C3%A9u_Stadium" title="Santiago Bernabéu Stadium">Santiago Bernabéu Stadium</a>, similarly to the previous signings of <a href="/wiki/Kak%C3%A1" title="Kaká">Kaká</a> and Cristiano Ronaldo.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Benzema made his Real Madrid debut on 20 July in the club's opening <a href="/wiki/Pre-season" class="mw-redirect" title="Pre-season">pre-season</a> <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game" title="Exhibition game">friendly</a> against <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Irish</a> club <a href="/wiki/Shamrock_Rovers_F.C." title="Shamrock Rovers F.C.">Shamrock Rovers</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a>, appearing as a half-time substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> He scored the lone goal in the club's 1–0 win, scoring in the 87th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> On 24 August, Benzema netted two goals in Real Madrid's 4–0 victory over Norwegian club Rosenborg in an annual friendly tournament organized for the <a href="/wiki/Trofeo_Santiago_Bernab%C3%A9u" title="Trofeo Santiago Bernabéu">Santiago Bernabeu Trophy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> The goals brought his total tally in the pre-season with Real Madrid to five, making him the joint top scorer alongside fellow striker <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_(footballer)" title="Raúl (footballer)">Raúl</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema made his league debut for Madrid on 29 August 2009 against <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_de_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo de La Coruña">Deportivo La Coruña</a>. He started the match, but was substituted out in the second half as Madrid won 3–2.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> A month later, he scored his first goal for the club in a 5–0 victory against newly promoted <a href="/wiki/Xerez_CD" title="Xerez CD">Xerez</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> After missing the mid-week match against <a href="/wiki/Villarreal_CF" title="Villarreal CF">Villarreal</a>, against <a href="/wiki/CD_Tenerife" title="CD Tenerife">Tenerife</a> at the weekend, Benzema scored his first double for Madrid in a 3–0 home victory.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> He made his Champions League debut for the club on 30 September in a group stage tie against Marseille.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> In the match, Benzema assisted on a Cristiano Ronaldo goal.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> After failing to score a goal in the month of October, in the team's first match in November against <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> club <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> in the Champions League, Benzema scored the opener to give Madrid a 1–0 lead. His goal was later cancelled out by a <a href="/wiki/Ronaldinho" title="Ronaldinho">Ronaldinho</a> penalty.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> On 7 November, in the <i><a href="/wiki/El_Derbi_madrile%C3%B1o" class="mw-redirect" title="El Derbi madrileño">El Derbi madrileño</a></i> against <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>, Benzema assisted on Madrid's second goal, scored by <a href="/wiki/Marcelo_(footballer,_born_1988)" title="Marcelo (footballer, born 1988)">Marcelo</a>. Madrid won the match 3–2.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Benzema_-_Rodriguez.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Benzema_-_Rodriguez.jpg/220px-Benzema_-_Rodriguez.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Benzema_-_Rodriguez.jpg/330px-Benzema_-_Rodriguez.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Benzema_-_Rodriguez.jpg/440px-Benzema_-_Rodriguez.jpg 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="602" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Benzema_-_Rodriguez.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema playing against Marseille in a 2009 Champions League match.</div></div></div>
<p>In late November, Benzema began appearing mainly as a substitute as manager <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Pellegrini" title="Manuel Pellegrini">Manuel Pellegrini</a> preferred <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Higua%C3%ADn" title="Gonzalo Higuaín">Gonzalo Higuaín</a> in the lead striker role. To coincide with his benching, the striker was also being criticized by the Spanish media for his under-performance and difficulties settling in the country as he had not yet begun learning the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish language</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> He was even declared the "new <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Anelka" title="Nicolas Anelka">Anelka</a>" by a Spanish newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Marca_(newspaper)" title="Marca (newspaper)">Marca</a></i> blogger, referring to former Real Madrid striker Nicolas Anelka who had a tumultuous year at the club before being sold.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Benzema was defended by his compatriot Zinedine Zidane, who admitted "after two months, I was also criticized" and that Benzema was "a talented player and talented players in Madrid must win".<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 5 December, Benzema appeared as a substitute for <a href="/wiki/Rafael_van_der_Vaart" title="Rafael van der Vaart">Rafael van der Vaart</a> and scored the third goal in a 6–0 romp of <a href="/wiki/UD_Almer%C3%ADa" title="UD Almería">Almería</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> The day after the match against Almería, Benzema responded to the criticism by stating, "I am totally integrated and very happy at Real Madrid," and, "Yes, I have improved my adaptation. I have a new home and I'm learning Spanish to understand myself better with my teammates."<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> After nearly a month coming off of the bench, he started alongside Higuaín away to <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a> on 12 December and responded by assisting on one of Higuaín's two goals.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> A week later, Benzema returned to the bench. On his 22nd birthday, he scored in a 6–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/Real_Zaragoza" title="Real Zaragoza">Real Zaragoza</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> Following an injury to Higuaín in early January 2010, Pellegrini inserted Benzema back into the starting lineup.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> After failing to score in his first two starts in the absence of Higuaín, against Deportivo La Coruña on 30 January, he scored a double in an important 3–1 away win.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> Following the return of Higuaín, Benzema was relegated back to a substitute's role and finished the campaign by making eight consecutive appearances off the bench. Included in one of those appearances was his final goal of the season against <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a> in a 5–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.9311:_First-team_mainstay"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010–11:_First-team_mainstay">2010–11: First-team mainstay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2010–11: First-team mainstay">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Benzema_Villarreal.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Benzema_Villarreal.jpg/220px-Benzema_Villarreal.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Benzema_Villarreal.jpg/330px-Benzema_Villarreal.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Benzema_Villarreal.jpg/440px-Benzema_Villarreal.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2589" data-file-height="1733" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Benzema_Villarreal.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema playing in a league match against Villarreal</div></div></div>
<p>Ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_La_Liga" title="2010–11 La Liga">2010–11 season</a>, Benzema switched to the number 9 shirt as Real Madrid were under the tutelage of new incoming manager <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a>. The striker immediately drew the ire of Mourinho who declared to reporters during a pre-season media session that "Benzema must understand that he is extremely talented, but that in itself is not enough", while also stating that "[Madrid] need a striker who is sparky, not one that is listless".<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Mourinho sentiments were later echoed by incoming France national team coach <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Blanc" title="Laurent Blanc">Laurent Blanc</a> who acknowledged that Benzema was "not used to working".<sup id="cite_ref-Mourinho_plans_to_keep_Benzema_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mourinho_plans_to_keep_Benzema-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> Blanc also stated that the striker needed to shed weight in order to fulfill his potential.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to Mourinho preferring Ronaldo and Higuaín as his forwards,<sup id="cite_ref-Mourinho_plans_to_keep_Benzema_97-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mourinho_plans_to_keep_Benzema-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> Benzema began the campaign as a substitute coming off the bench in the team's opening league match of the season against <a href="/wiki/RCD_Mallorca" title="RCD Mallorca">Mallorca</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> Following the September international break, he made his first start in a 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/CA_Osasuna" title="CA Osasuna">Osasuna</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> On 21 September, Benzema made a substitute appearance and scored his first goal of the season in a 3–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/RCD_Espanyol" title="RCD Espanyol">Espanyol</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Afterwards, the striker failed to score a domestic goal for nearly two months. The striker did assist on goals in back-to-back weeks against <a href="/wiki/H%C3%A9rcules_CF" title="Hércules CF">Hércules</a> in the league and Milan in the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:La_alegr%C3%ADa_del_gol,_Benzema.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/La_alegr%C3%ADa_del_gol%2C_Benzema.jpg/220px-La_alegr%C3%ADa_del_gol%2C_Benzema.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/La_alegr%C3%ADa_del_gol%2C_Benzema.jpg/330px-La_alegr%C3%ADa_del_gol%2C_Benzema.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/La_alegr%C3%ADa_del_gol%2C_Benzema.jpg/440px-La_alegr%C3%ADa_del_gol%2C_Benzema.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="665" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:La_alegr%C3%ADa_del_gol,_Benzema.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">celebrating a goal</a> against Espanyol in La Liga.</div></div></div>
<p>On 10 November, Benzema scored his second goal of the campaign against <a href="/wiki/Real_Murcia" title="Real Murcia">Real Murcia</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Copa_del_Rey" title="2010–11 Copa del Rey">2010–11 edition</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> In late November, Benzema was inserted into the starting eleven following a severe back injury to Higuaín, along with the team's lack of senior strikers. In his first match since being inserted into the starting lineup permanently, he scored his first Champions League goal of the season in a group stage fixture against <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Dutch</a> club <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> In Madrid's final group stage tie against French outfit <a href="/wiki/AJ_Auxerre" title="AJ Auxerre">Auxerre</a>, Benzema scored his first <a href="/wiki/Hat_trick" class="mw-redirect" title="Hat trick">hat trick</a> for the club in a 4–0 win. The first goal he scored was Real Madrid's 300th goal in the Champions League era.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> Two weeks later, Benzema converted another hat trick, this time in an 8–0 thrashing of <a href="/wiki/Levante_UD" title="Levante UD">Levante</a> in the Copa del Rey.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> In the team's first fixture of the 2011 calendar year, he assisted on the game-winning goal scored by Ronaldo in a 3–2 win over <a href="/wiki/Getafe_CF" title="Getafe CF">Getafe</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> In late January, for the first time in his Real Madrid career, Benzema scored goals in back-to-back matches. On 23 January, he scored the only goal in a 1–0 win at home against Mallorca.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Benzema repeated his efforts scoring the only goal in a win over <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> in the first leg of the team's Copa del Rey semi-final tie.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> Real Madrid later advanced to its 37th Copa del Rey final in club history after beating Sevilla 2–0 in the second leg.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Emmanuel_Adebayor" title="Emmanuel Adebayor">Emmanuel Adebayor</a> on loan, Benzema went unused in two consecutive league matches in February 2011. He returned to the starting lineup on 19 February and embarked on a run in which he scored ten goals in eight matches. Included in those ten goals were doubles in three straight matches against <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A1laga_CF" title="Málaga CF">Málaga</a>, <a href="/wiki/Racing_de_Santander" title="Racing de Santander">Racing de Santander</a> and Hércules, as well as a goal in the first leg of Madrid's Round of 16 tie against former club Lyon.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> The strike against his hometown club was the 100th goal of his professional career, and also the first goal for Real Madrid at the Stade de Gerland in six years, though despite the honours associated with netting the goal, Benzema did not celebrate out of respect for his former club.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Benzema_dribbles.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Benzema_dribbles.jpg/220px-Benzema_dribbles.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="145" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Benzema_dribbles.jpg/330px-Benzema_dribbles.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Benzema_dribbles.jpg/440px-Benzema_dribbles.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="677" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Benzema_dribbles.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema playing in a league match against Almería.</div></div></div>
<p>On 19 March, he scored the opener in the <i>El Derbi madrileño</i> as Real Madrid went on to win the match 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> Despite his form, Benzema appeared in only one of the four highly anticipated matches against <i><a href="/wiki/El_Cl%C3%A1sico" title="El Clásico">El Clásico</a></i> rivals <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, in which the two clubs met in the league, the <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_del_Rey_Final" title="2011 Copa del Rey Final">2011 Copa del Rey Final</a> and the Champions League knockout stage. In between those clashes, on 23 April 2011, Benzema scored a goal and assisted on another in a 6–3 win over Valencia.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> On 30 April, he scored a goal in the team's 3–2 loss to Real Zaragoza.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> It was the only match of the campaign that Real Madrid loss, in which Benzema scored. To close out the campaign, Benzema scored another double in an 8–1 win over Almería.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> He finished the campaign second on the team behind Ronaldo with 26 goals as Real Madrid captured the Copa del Rey giving Benzema his first honour with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> For his performances during the campaign, particularly during the second half, Benzema was praised by Mourinho, club officials <a href="/wiki/Florentino_P%C3%A9rez" title="Florentino Pérez">Florentino Pérez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Emilio_Butrague%C3%B1o" title="Emilio Butragueño">Emilio Butragueño</a>, as well as national team manager Laurent Blanc.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9312:_First_La_Liga_championship"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2011–12:_First_La_Liga_championship">2011–12: First La Liga championship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2011–12: First La Liga championship">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Prior to the start of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_La_Liga" title="2011–12 La Liga">2011–12 season</a>, Benzema, taking the advice of compatriots Blanc and Zidane,<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> ventured to <a href="/wiki/Merano" title="Merano">Merano</a>, Italy, to attend a high performance clinic where he underwent treatment to reduce his weight.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_weight_127-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_weight-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> The spell at the clinic was ultimately a success after the striker arrived at pre-season 8 kilograms (18&#160;lb) lighter.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_weight_127-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_weight-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> While at the clinic, Benzema also underwent physical training to build up his <a href="/wiki/Muscle_mass" class="mw-redirect" title="Muscle mass">muscle mass</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_weight_127-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_weight-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> The striker was impressive in the pre-season scoring eight goals in seven matches.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> His performances during the pre-season resulted in Mourinho naming him the starting lead striker for the new campaign. Mourinho was later credited with Benzema's transformation,<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> but denied full responsibility and, instead, gave credit to the striker himself.<sup id="cite_ref-mourinho_benzema_130-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mourinho_benzema-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema made his 2011–12 competitive debut for Madrid in the first leg of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2011 Supercopa de España">2011 Supercopa de España</a> against Barcelona. In the match, he started and assisted on the opening goal of the match, scored by <a href="/wiki/Mesut_%C3%96zil" title="Mesut Özil">Mesut Özil</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> In the second leg, with Madrid trailing 4–3 on aggregate late in the match, Benzema scored the equalizing goal to even the tie at 4–4. However, six minutes later, a <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> strike gave Barcelona the supercup.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> Benzema made his league debut for Madrid in the team's 6–0 away win over Real Zaragoza.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> In the team's next league match two weeks later against Getafe, Benzema scored a double in a 4–2 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> After going scoreless in three consecutive league matches, he scored his third league goal of the campaign against <a href="/wiki/Rayo_Vallecano" title="Rayo Vallecano">Rayo Vallecano</a> in a 4–2 win.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> In the team's ensuing match against Ajax in the Champions League, Benzema scored Madrid's third goal in a 3–0 home win.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> He also assisted on the opener, which was scored by Ronaldo.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> In the club's next Champions League match against Lyon, Benzema scored again netting the opener. He also turned provider for the second consecutive match assisting on a goal by <a href="/wiki/Sami_Khedira" title="Sami Khedira">Sami Khedira</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> Madrid won the match 4–0.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:30%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Benzema deserves full credit for his transformation. He had some help from me, from his teammates and from <i>Zizou</i>, but he deserves the credit."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><small>—<a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a>, on Benzema's successful progression in 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-mourinho_benzema_130-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mourinho_benzema-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> </small></cite>
</p>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a href="/wiki/File:KarimBenzema.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/KarimBenzema.jpg/180px-KarimBenzema.jpg" decoding="async" width="180" height="211" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/KarimBenzema.jpg/270px-KarimBenzema.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/KarimBenzema.jpg/360px-KarimBenzema.jpg 2x" data-file-width="362" data-file-height="424" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:KarimBenzema.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema training ahead of a Champions League match in 2012.</div></div></div>
<p>In November 2011, Benzema scored five goals; three in the league and two in Europe. In the league, he converted his three goals in wins over Osasuna and Valencia, while he scored his two Champions League goals in a 6–2 group stage win over <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatian</a> club <a href="/wiki/GNK_Dinamo_Zagreb" title="GNK Dinamo Zagreb">Dinamo Zagreb</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> On 10 December 2011, Benzema scored the opener in Madrid's 3–1 defeat to Barcelona in the <i>El Clásico</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> The goal, scored just 21 seconds into the match, was the fastest goal ever scored in a match between the two rivals.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> Three days after his record-breaking goal, for his performances during the 2011 calendar year, Benzema was named the <i>France Football</i> <a href="/wiki/France_Football#French_Player_of_the_Year" title="France Football">French Player of the Year</a>, beating out Barcelona defender <a href="/wiki/Eric_Abidal" title="Eric Abidal">Eric Abidal</a> and Lyon goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Lloris" title="Hugo Lloris">Hugo Lloris</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> He became only the second French player based in Spain to win the award, and also the second Real Madrid player to capture it. Zidane was the first to achieve both honorable mentions. Benzema expressed gratitude at winning the award, stating, "It is a pleasure to win an individual trophy. When I see the previous winners&#160;– Zidane, <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Henry</a> and other major players&#160;– it makes me proud to join them on the list."<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> In the team's next match after winning the award, against Sevilla, Benzema assisted on two goals in a 6–2 triumph.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema opened the 2012 portion of the campaign in positive form. He scored goals against <a href="/wiki/Granada_CF" title="Granada CF">Granada</a> and Málaga.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> Benzema scored against the latter club in the Copa del Rey in each leg of the Round of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> The 4–2 aggregate win advanced Real Madrid to the quarter-finals where the club faced Barcelona. After failing to score in the first leg, which ended 2–1 in favour of <i>Barça</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> in the second leg on 25 January 2012, Benzema scored his third goal of the season against the <i>Blaugrana</i>, but Madrid failed to win the tie losing 4–3 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> On 12 February, Benzema scored his first league goal in over a month against Levante.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> A week later, he scored a double in a 4–0 shutout of Racing Santander.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> On 24 March, Benzema scored two goals in a league win over Real Sociedad.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> The two goals made him the top French scorer in La Liga history surpassing Zidane.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Benzema scored another double in a 3–0 first leg away win over <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cypriot</a> club <a href="/wiki/APOEL_FC" title="APOEL FC">APOEL</a> in the Champions League quarter-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> On 29 April, Benzema put in a masterpiece performance scoring two goals and assisting on another in a 3–0 win over Sevilla. The double was his seventh of the season and allowed Madrid to close in on its first <i>Primera Division</i> title in four years.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> <i>Los Blancos</i> captured their 32nd league title the following week cruising to a 3–0 win over Athletic Bilbao.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup> Benzema appeared as a second-half substitute in the match.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9316:_Sustained_continental_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2012–16:_Sustained_continental_success">2012–16: Sustained continental success</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2012–16: Sustained continental success">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On the first matchday of the UEFA Champions League, Benzema scored an equalizer against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> in 3–2 win at Santiago Bernabéu. On 4 October 2012, Benzema scored a bicycle kick goal off a cross by Kaká in a 4–1 win against Ajax in <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> On 18 December 2012, one day before his 25th birthday, his fine form saw him earn the award for best French footballer of 2012, for the second year running.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> On 2 March 2013, Benzema opened the scoring against Barcelona in the league game at the Santiago Bernabéu. Real went on to win the game 2–1, the second time they beat Barcelona in a week. On 30 April 2013, Benzema scored one goal and assisted to <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ramos" title="Sergio Ramos">Sergio Ramos</a> against Dortmund.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema started the 2013–14 season by scoring in a 2–1 win over Real Betis at the Santiago Bernabéu.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> He scored again one week later in a 1–0 away over Granada, assisted by Cristiano Ronaldo.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> After four matches without scoring (two with Real Madrid and two with France), he returned to goal-scoring form by netting twice in a 6–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K._(football)" title="Galatasaray S.K. (football)">Galatasaray</a> in <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> On 18 January 2014, he scored his 100th goal for Madrid in a 5–0 victory at <a href="/wiki/Real_Betis" title="Real Betis">Real Betis</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> On 23 March, Benzema scored two goals against fierce rivals Barcelona in <i>El Clásico</i> at the Bernabéu from two crosses by <a href="/wiki/%C3%81ngel_Di_Mar%C3%ADa" title="Ángel Di María">Ángel Di María</a>, taking his goal tally in La Liga to 17 goals, though Barcelona won the match 4–3.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:192px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Karim_Benzema_vs._FC_Schalke_04_(16647992937).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Karim_Benzema_vs._FC_Schalke_04_%2816647992937%29.jpg/190px-Karim_Benzema_vs._FC_Schalke_04_%2816647992937%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="190" height="300" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Karim_Benzema_vs._FC_Schalke_04_%2816647992937%29.jpg/285px-Karim_Benzema_vs._FC_Schalke_04_%2816647992937%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Karim_Benzema_vs._FC_Schalke_04_%2816647992937%29.jpg/380px-Karim_Benzema_vs._FC_Schalke_04_%2816647992937%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2738" data-file-height="4327" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Karim_Benzema_vs._FC_Schalke_04_(16647992937).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema during the 2014–15 season</div></div></div>
<p>Benzema was part of Real Madrid's starting eleven in the <a href="/wiki/2014_Copa_del_Rey_Final" title="2014 Copa del Rey Final">2014 Copa del Rey Final</a> on 16 April at the <a href="/wiki/Mestalla_Stadium" title="Mestalla Stadium">Mestalla Stadium</a>, and assisted Di María's opening goal before <a href="/wiki/Gareth_Bale" title="Gareth Bale">Gareth Bale</a> hit the winner for Madrid in a 2–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> One week later, on 23 April, Benzema scored the only goal of the game to win the first leg of a Champions League semi-final against Bayern Munich, 1–0.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> The club went on to win the <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2014 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a> in May. Real Madrid's attacking trio of Bale, Benzema and Cristiano, dubbed "BBC", finished the season with 97 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 August 2014, Real Madrid announced that Benzema had signed a new five-year deal that will keep him at the club until 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> On 12 August 2014, Benzema played the whole 90 minutes in Real Madrid's 2–0 win against Sevilla in <a href="/wiki/Cardiff" title="Cardiff">Cardiff</a> to claim the <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2014 UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a>. On 16 September, Benzema scored Real Madrid's 1,000th goal in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_competitions" title="UEFA competitions">European competition</a> after netting a goal in a 5–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/FC_Basel" title="FC Basel">FC Basel</a> in the first match of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2014–15 UEFA Champions League group stage">Champions League group stage</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> He scored the winning goal in Real Madrid's 2–1 away victory against <a href="/wiki/PFC_Ludogorets_Razgrad" title="PFC Ludogorets Razgrad">Ludogorets Razgrad</a> in the Champions League after coming on as a second-half substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> The next weekend, he scored a brace in the 5–0 victory against Athletic Bilbao in La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup> In 2014, Benzema won France Football's award for <a href="/wiki/French_Player_of_the_Year" title="French Player of the Year">French Player of the Year</a> for the third time; only <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a> has won this award on more occasions.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema was chosen as <a href="/wiki/La_Liga_Player_of_the_Month" title="La Liga Player of the Month">La Liga Player of the Month</a> for October 2014, with his manager <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ancelotti" title="Carlo Ancelotti">Carlo Ancelotti</a> winning <a href="/wiki/La_Liga_Manager_of_the_Month" title="La Liga Manager of the Month">the equivalent award</a>. He scored three of Real Madrid's 13 goals of the month, in which they won three matches and only conceded just one goal.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> On 8 December 2015, Benzema scored a hat trick in an 8–0 thrashing against <a href="/wiki/Malm%C3%B6_FF" title="Malmö FF">Malmö FF</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> On 20 December, he scored another hat trick in a 10–2 victory over Rayo Vallecano.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup> He was a regular starter when the team won the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">2015–16 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9320:_Third_league_title.2C_fourth_European_Cup"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–20:_Third_league_title,_fourth_European_Cup">2016–20: Third league title, fourth European Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 2016–20: Third league title, fourth European Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Shahter-Reak_M_2015_(15).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2815%29.jpg/180px-Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2815%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="180" height="233" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2815%29.jpg/270px-Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2815%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2815%29.jpg/360px-Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2815%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="374" data-file-height="485" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Shahter-Reak_M_2015_(15).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema with <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid" class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid">Real Madrid</a> in 2015</div></div></div>
<p>In December 2016, Benzema was called up in Real Madrid's <a href="/wiki/2016_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_squads" title="2016 FIFA Club World Cup squads">squad</a> for <a href="/wiki/2016_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2016 FIFA Club World Cup">2016 FIFA Club World Cup</a> in Japan.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-final match against <a href="/wiki/Club_Am%C3%A9rica" title="Club América">América</a> on 15 December, Benzema scored in the last moments of the first half, helping the team to progress in the final by winning 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2016_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2016 FIFA Club World Cup Final">final</a> three days later against <a href="/wiki/Kashima_Antlers" title="Kashima Antlers">Kashima Antlers</a>, Benzema opened the score in the 9th minute, and also assisted Ronaldo's second goal, as Real Madrid won 4–2 in extra time after the regular time finished 2–2 to claim their second title.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup> It was Benzema's tenth title with Real Madrid, and finished the competition as joint-second topscorer with two goals in two matches.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 February 2017, in the first leg of <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">2016–17 UEFA Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">round of 16</a> against <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a>, Benzema scored Real Madrid's first goal in an eventual 3–1 home win, which was his 51st goal in this competition, overtaking <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a> on the list of <a href="/wiki/European_Cup_and_UEFA_Champions_League_records_and_statistics#All-time_top_scorers" title="European Cup and UEFA Champions League records and statistics">all-time Champions League top scorers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> It was his first goal in six matches and for this performance he was voted Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> He was a regular starter, and scored the last goal of the season which gave him eleven for the campaign, when Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_La_Liga" title="2016–17 La Liga">2016–17 La Liga</a><sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">2016–17 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 20 September 2017, Benzema signed a contract extension that will keep him at the club until 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> Later on 6 March of the following year, Benzema made his 100th UEFA Champions League appearance by playing in the 2–1 win at <a href="/wiki/Parc_des_Princes" title="Parc des Princes">Parc des Princes</a> against <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> in the second leg of <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League#Round_of_16" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">2017–18 UEFA Champions League round of 16</a> as Real Madrid progressed to the next round 5–2 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> Benzema played his 400th match in all competitions for Real Madrid on 31 March in the 3–0 win at <a href="/wiki/UD_Las_Palmas" title="UD Las Palmas">Las Palmas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captaining</a> the team and netting the second goal with a penalty.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> On 1 May 2018, Benzema scored twice in a 2–2 draw against <a href="/wiki/Bayern_Munich" class="mw-redirect" title="Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> in the return leg of the <a href="/wiki/2017-18_UEFA_Champions_League#Semi_Final" class="mw-redirect" title="2017-18 UEFA Champions League">2017–18 UEFA Champions League semi-final</a>, as Real progressed to the final on a 4–3 aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> On 26 May, Benzema scored the first goal of the match in <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Champions League Final">2018 UEFA Champions League Final</a> by intercepting <a href="/wiki/Loris_Karius" title="Loris Karius">Loris Karius</a>'s throw in a 3–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>, when Madrid won their third consecutive and 13th overall Champions League title.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 November 2018, Benzema scored a brace in the 5–0 win at <a href="/wiki/FC_Viktoria_Plze%C5%88" title="FC Viktoria Plze">Viktoria Plze</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League group stage">UEFA Champions League group stage</a>, reaching the 200th goal milestone with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup> He became only the seventh Real Madrid player to achieve the feat.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> He totaled three goals in six matches, all of them against Viktoria Plze, helping Real Madrid topping <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League#Group_G" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">Group G</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup> Later on 13 February of the following year, in the first leg of the competition's <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">round of 16</a>, Benzema scored the opener of a 2–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup> reaching 60 Champions League goals, becoming only the fourth player to do so.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Benzema scored Real Madrid's first competitive goal of the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2019–20 Real Madrid CF season">2019–20 season</a> on 17 August in the 3–1 away win over Celta Vigo in the opening <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> match.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> Later, on 6 November, he scored a brace in Real Madrid's 6–0 crushing of <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K._(football)" title="Galatasaray S.K.
