(football)">Galatasaray</a>, achieving two new milestones: he become the second player after <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> to score in 15 consecutive Champions League seasons and also the third Real Madrid player to score 50 goals in the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup> His performances were praised by manager <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>, who called him a legend and also compared him with Cristiano Ronaldo.<sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, in the next league match, he scored a first-half brace in a 4–0 win at <a href="/wiki/SD_Eibar" title="SD Eibar">Eibar</a>, overtaking <a href="/wiki/Ferenc_Pusk%C3%A1s" title="Ferenc Puskás">Ferenc Puskás</a> as the club's 6th all-time goalscorer in La Liga with 157 goals from 323 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>In February 2020, Benzema extended his contract with Real Madrid until 2022.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup> On 1 March, he made his 500th appearance for Real Madrid in a 2–0 home win over Barcelona in El Clásico, becoming the fourteenth player in the club's history to achieve this milestone.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the season, Real Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_La_Liga" title="2019–20 La Liga">2019–20 La Liga</a>, while scoring over 20 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-Liga_210-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liga-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 2020–21 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 4 October 2020, Benzema scored his 250th goal for Real Madrid in all competitions, in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Levante_UD" title="Levante UD">Levante UD</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup> On 27 October, he scored a goal in a 2–2 draw against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, to become the second player in history after Lionel Messi to score in 16 consecutive Champions League seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup> On 9 December, he scored a brace in a 2–0 win over Borussia Mönchengladbach to reach the Champions League knockout stages.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth">Youth</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Youth">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Benzema is a former <a href="/wiki/France_national_youth_football_team" title="France national youth football team">France youth international</a> having earned caps at all levels for which he was eligible, excluding the <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-16_football_team" title="France national under-16 football team">under-16 team</a>. He is a member of the group, commonly known in France as the <i>Génération 1987</i>, a youth class that produced current internationals <a href="/wiki/Hatem_Ben_Arfa" title="Hatem Ben Arfa">Hatem Ben Arfa</a>, <a href="/wiki/J%C3%A9r%C3%A9my_M%C3%A9nez" title="Jérémy Ménez">Jérémy Ménez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Samir_Nasri" title="Samir Nasri">Samir Nasri</a>, alongside himself.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup> Benzema was the last of the four to make his youth international debut under coach <a href="/wiki/Philippe_Bergeroo" title="Philippe Bergeroo">Philippe Bergeroo</a> and officially joined the team ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2004_UEFA_European_Under-17_Championship" title="2004 UEFA European Under-17 Championship">2004 UEFA European Under-17 Championship</a> that was played on home soil. In the competition, he appeared in two matches. On his tournament debut, Benzema scored the opening goal in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland_national_under-17_football_team" title="Northern Ireland national under-17 football team">Northern Ireland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup> His lone other appearance in the competition was in a 1–0 group stage win over <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_under-17_football_team" title="Spain national under-17 football team">Spain</a> as France went on to win the tournament defeated the same team in the final.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema was a regular starter in the team at <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-18_football_team" title="France national under-18 football team">under-18</a> level. He made his debut with the team at a local tournament in the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a>. Benzema scored his first goal at under-18 level in the competition against <a href="/wiki/Poland_national_under-18_football_team" title="Poland national under-18 football team">Poland</a> in the team's final group stage match.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup> In the final against <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic_national_under-18_football_team" title="Czech Republic national under-18 football team">the hosts</a>, he scored the opening goal in a 2–0 win as France were declared champions of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup> On 30 September 2004, Benzema was one of three goalscorers in France's 3–0 away win over Norway.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup> In the team's next match against Russia, he scored a double in a 3–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup> Due to France winning the 2004 U17 European title, the under-18 team was allowed participation in the <a href="/wiki/2005_UEFA%E2%80%93CAF_Meridian_Cup" title="2005 UEFA–CAF Meridian Cup">2005 Meridian Cup</a>. Benzema was called up to the team for the competition and played in all four matches, scoring a tournament-high five goals as France were crowned champions of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup> He opened the tournament by scoring two goals in a 7–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Cameroon_national_under-17_football_team" title="Cameroon national under-17 football team">Cameroon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup> After going scoreless in the team's next match against <a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone_national_under-17_football_team" title="Sierra Leone national under-17 football team">Sierra Leone</a>, Benzema responded by scoring a goal in a shutout victory over <a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_under-17_football_team" title="Nigeria national under-17 football team">Nigeria</a> and netting another double in a 4–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Egypt_national_under-17_football_team" title="Egypt national under-17 football team">Egypt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup> On 19 May 2005, in the team's final match of the season against <a href="/wiki/Slovakia_national_under-18_football_team" title="Slovakia national under-18 football team">Slovakia</a>, Benzema scored all four goals in a 4–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup> He finished the under-18 campaign with 18 appearances and a team-high 14 goals and was, subsequently, praised by Bergeroo who, following the campaign, declared that Benzema was "quite efficient".<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The foursome of Benzema, Ben Arfa, Ménez and Nasri returned to international play together for <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-19_football_team" title="France national under-19 football team">under-19</a> duty. The four were joined by <a href="/wiki/Issiar_Dia" title="Issiar Dia">Issiar Dia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Matuidi" title="Blaise Matuidi">Blaise Matuidi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Serge_Gakp%C3%A9" title="Serge Gakpé">Serge Gakpé</a> with the objective of winning the <a href="/wiki/2006_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2006 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2006 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</a>. The team opened the campaign with two friendly matches against <a href="/wiki/Norway_national_under-19_football_team" title="Norway national under-19 football team">Norway</a>. Over the course of the two matches, Benzema scored one goal, which came in the first match, a 4–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup> In the first round of qualification for the UEFA-sanctioned tournament, he scored his only goal in the final group match against <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_under-19_football_team" title="Austria national under-19 football team">Austria</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup> France won the match 2–0, which resulted in the team progressing to the Elite Round.<sup id="cite_ref-231" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-231">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup> In the ensuing round, France were placed in a relatively easy group alongside <a href="/wiki/Scotland_national_under-19_football_team" title="Scotland national under-19 football team">Scotland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria_national_under-19_football_team" title="Bulgaria national under-19 football team">Bulgaria</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Belarus_national_under-19_football_team" title="Belarus national under-19 football team">Belarus</a>. In the opening group game against Bulgaria, Benzema scored a double converting a penalty and scoring in play as France won 4–0.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup> Both of his goals were scored within a minute of each other.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup> After surprisingly drawing 0–0 with Belarus, France faced Scotland in the final group stage match. Benzema opened the scoring in the 11th minute, but his goal was cancelled out by <a href="/wiki/Steven_Fletcher_(footballer)" title="Steven Fletcher (footballer)">Steven Fletcher</a> in the second half.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup> The match ultimately finished 1–1 and, despite finishing the round undefeated, France were eliminated after being beaten on points by the <i>Scots</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema made his <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-21_football_team" title="France national under-21 football team">under-21</a> debut for <i>Les Espoirs</i> under coach <a href="/wiki/Ren%C3%A9_Girard_(footballer)" title="René Girard (footballer)">René Girard</a> in the team's first match following the <a href="/wiki/2006_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2006 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">2006 UEFA European Under-21 Championship</a> against <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_under-21_football_team" title="Belgium national under-21 football team">Belgium</a>. He started the match and was replaced at half-time by <a href="/wiki/Yoann_Gourcuff" title="Yoann Gourcuff">Yoann Gourcuff</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup> He featured in <a href="/wiki/2007_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship_qualification" title="2007 UEFA European Under-21 Championship qualification">qualification matches</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2007_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2007 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">2007 UEFA European Under-21 Championship</a> and appeared as a starter and substitute in the first leg and second leg, respectively, of the team's surprising defeat to Israel in the qualifying playoffs.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;239&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">&#91;240&#93;</a></sup> Despite still being eligible to represent the under-21 team until 2009, his appearance in the second leg defeat to Israel was Benzema's last with the team and he finished his under-21 career with five appearances and no goals. Prior to representing France at senior international level, Benzema was courted by the <a href="/wiki/Algerian_Football_Federation" title="Algerian Football Federation">Algerian Football Federation</a> (FAF) who sought for the player to represent <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> at senior international level. In December 2006, the striker was approached by former federation president Hamid Haddadj and then-national team coach <a href="/wiki/Jean-Michel_Cavalli" title="Jean-Michel Cavalli">Jean-Michel Cavalli</a>, but turned down the invitation citing his desire to continue his international career with France.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;241&#93;</a></sup> Benzema later told French <a href="/wiki/Radio_station" class="mw-redirect" title="Radio station">radio station</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Radio_Monte_Carlo" title="Radio Monte Carlo">Radio Monte Carlo</a></i> "Algeria is my parents' country and it is in my heart, but football-wise, I will only play for the French national team".<sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior">Senior</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Senior">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2008">Euro 2008</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Euro 2008">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:KBenzema.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/KBenzema.jpg/170px-KBenzema.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/KBenzema.jpg/255px-KBenzema.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/KBenzema.jpg/340px-KBenzema.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1361" data-file-height="1816" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:KBenzema.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema playing for France in April 2008</div></div></div>
<p>Benzema was called up for the first time to the senior national team by <a href="/wiki/Raymond_Domenech" title="Raymond Domenech">Raymond Domenech</a> on 9 November 2006 for the team's friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Greece_national_football_team" title="Greece national football team">Greece</a> that would be played on 15 November. Benzema described the call-up as "a reward", while also stating "I am pleased, of course, me and my family. A (the senior national team), is the national team's highest honor".<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">&#91;243&#93;</a></sup> Two days before the match, he was forced to withdraw from the team due to a thigh injury, which he suffered while playing domestically for Lyon.<sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">&#91;244&#93;</a></sup> After failing to make the squad for the team's February 2007 match against <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>, Benzema returned to the team in March for a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2008 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2008 qualifying</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Lithuania_national_football_team" title="Lithuania national football team">Lithuania</a> and a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austria</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">&#91;245&#93;</a></sup> After failing to appear in the qualifier, he made his international debut on 28 March 2007 against Austria. Benzema appeared as a half-time substitute for <a href="/wiki/Djibril_Ciss%C3%A9" title="Djibril Cissé">Djibril Cissé</a> and scored the only goal of the match after a free-kick from Samir Nasri.<sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246">&#91;246&#93;</a></sup> On 13 October, Benzema scored a double in a 6–0 win against the <a href="/wiki/Faroe_Islands_national_football_team" title="Faroe Islands national football team">Faroe Islands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247">&#91;247&#93;</a></sup> After appearing regularly in the team for the rest of the 2007–08 season, he was named to the 23-man squad to participate in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">UEFA Euro 2008</a>.
</p><p>Benzema made his debut in the competition on 9 June 2008 in the team's opening match against <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a>. Benzema started the match, but was substituted out for Nasri in the second half after a frustrating performance.<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">&#91;248&#93;</a></sup> The match finished 0–0 and Benzema was, subsequently, criticized by the French media for his performance with newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Point" title="Le Point">Le Point</a></i> declaring that Benzema was "unrecognizable" and that he "symbolized the impotence of France in the attack".<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">&#91;249&#93;</a></sup> The newspaper also cited his lack of international experience for his subdued performance. In the team's next group game against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a>, Benzema played no part in the 4–1 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">&#91;250&#93;</a></sup> He returned to the team in its final group game against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a> and was given a place in the starting lineup.<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251">&#91;251&#93;</a></sup> However, France lost 2–0 and were eliminated from the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252">&#91;252&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In November 2008, Benzema, among several other young players in the team, was accused of being insolent during the team's campaign at the European Championship. The accusation came from international teammate <a href="/wiki/William_Gallas" title="William Gallas">William Gallas</a> who inserted the charge in his autobiography. Though most of Gallas' accusations were directed at Nasri,<sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253">&#91;253&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254">&#91;254&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255">&#91;255&#93;</a></sup> during the competition, it was reported by newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Parisien" title="Le Parisien">Le Parisien</a></i> that several of the national team players described Benzema as "arrogant" and that the striker was scolded by <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfielder</a> <a href="/wiki/Claude_Mak%C3%A9l%C3%A9l%C3%A9" title="Claude Makélélé">Claude Makélélé</a> following the team's loss to the Netherlands.<sup id="cite_ref-256" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-256">&#91;256&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2010_World_Cup">2010 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 2010 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite the reports from after Euro 2008, Benzema remained a regular in the team and, ahead of <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2010 FIFA World Cup qualification">qualification</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a>, switched to the number ten shirt after previously wearing the number nine.<sup id="cite_ref-257" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-257">&#91;257&#93;</a></sup> In the team's first match following its elimination from Euro 2008, Benzema scored a goal in a 3–2 friendly win over <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a> in <a href="/wiki/Gothenburg" title="Gothenburg">Gothenburg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">&#91;258&#93;</a></sup> Two months later, he scored another goal in a 3–1 victory against <a href="/wiki/Tunisia_national_football_team" title="Tunisia national football team">Tunisia</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">&#91;259&#93;</a></sup> On 5 June 2009, Benzema converted the only goal of the match, a penalty shot, in a 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Turkey_national_football_team" title="Turkey national football team">Turkey</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_Gerland" title="Stade de Gerland">Stade de Gerland</a>, his home stadium.<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">&#91;260&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first World Cup qualification goals in victories over the Faroe Islands and Austria in October 2009. His cap against Austria would be his last of the Domenech era as he failed to make France's preliminary 30-man squad for the World Cup. Domenech cited Benzema's struggle for form with his new club Real Madrid, rather than his alleged involvement in a sex scandal as his reason for leaving the striker out.<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">&#91;261&#93;</a></sup> Prior to the list being unveiled, Benzema informed <i>Radio Monte Carlo</i> that if he was not selected he would be "very disappointed, but not killed" and "I will support the France team no matter what".<sup id="cite_ref-262" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-262">&#91;262&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2012">Euro 2012</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Euro 2012">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Karim_Benzema_Euro_2012_vs_Sweden_01.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Karim_Benzema_Euro_2012_vs_Sweden_01.jpg/170px-Karim_Benzema_Euro_2012_vs_Sweden_01.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Karim_Benzema_Euro_2012_vs_Sweden_01.jpg/255px-Karim_Benzema_Euro_2012_vs_Sweden_01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Karim_Benzema_Euro_2012_vs_Sweden_01.jpg/340px-Karim_Benzema_Euro_2012_vs_Sweden_01.jpg 2x" data-file-width="437" data-file-height="656" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Karim_Benzema_Euro_2012_vs_Sweden_01.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Benzema playing for France at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Following the World Cup, Benzema returned to the national team under the reign of new coach <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Blanc" title="Laurent Blanc">Laurent Blanc</a>. Blanc, an admirer of Benzema, sought to build the attack around the striker and, after going almost a year without representing France, Benzema made his return to the team in its 2–1 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Norway_national_football_team" title="Norway national football team">Norway</a> in <a href="/wiki/Oslo" title="Oslo">Oslo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263">&#91;263&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264">&#91;264&#93;</a></sup> Alongside Gourcuff, Benzema led the team in scoring in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_Group_D" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying Group D">qualifying</a> for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a> netting three. He scored his three goals in wins over <a href="/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina_national_football_team" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina national football team">Bosnia and Herzegovina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg_national_football_team" title="Luxembourg national football team">Luxembourg</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Albania_national_football_team" title="Albania national football team">Albania</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265">&#91;265&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266">&#91;266&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267">&#91;267&#93;</a></sup> On 17 November 2010, Benzema scored the opening goal in France's 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268">&#91;268&#93;</a></sup> In the team's next match against <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> in February 2011, he scored the only goal for France in a 1–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-269" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-269">&#91;269&#93;</a></sup> After appearing regularly in qualifying for UEFA Euro 2012, on 29 May 2012, Benzema was named to the squad to participate in the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270">&#91;270&#93;</a></sup> On 5 June, in the team's final warm-up friendly ahead of the European Championship, Benzema scored two goals in a 4–0 shutout win over <a href="/wiki/Estonia_national_football_team" title="Estonia national football team">Estonia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271">&#91;271&#93;</a></sup> At UEFA Euro 2012, Benzema started the team's opening match against England, which ended in a 1–1 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">&#91;272&#93;</a></sup> In the team's ensuing group stage match against the Ukraine, he assisted on both team goals in a 2–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">&#91;273&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_World_Cup">2014 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 2014 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 11 October 2013, Benzema scored his first goal for the France national team since June 2012 in a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_association_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Australia national association football team">Australia</a>, thus ending a scoring drought for his national team which had lasted 1,222 minutes. In that match played at the <a href="/wiki/Parc_des_Princes" title="Parc des Princes">Parc des Princes</a> stadium in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>, which France won 6–0, Benzema scored France's sixth and final goal in the 50th minute after turning home <a href="/wiki/Franck_Rib%C3%A9ry" title="Franck Ribéry">Franck Ribéry</a>'s left-wing cross.<sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">&#91;274&#93;</a></sup> In the second leg of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Second_Round" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Second Round">2014 World Cup qualification play-off</a> against <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_football_team" title="Ukraine national football team">Ukraine</a> held on 19 November 2013 at the Stade de France, Benzema scored France's second goal in the 34th minute to level the aggregate score at 2–2. Benzema scored his goal when he side-footed home after a huge scramble in the Ukrainian penalty box, although he was shown on television replays to be offside by almost one metre when the ball took a final touch off <a href="/wiki/Mathieu_Valbuena" title="Mathieu Valbuena">Mathieu Valbuena</a>'s chest. Benzema had four minutes earlier been denied a legitimate goal, the offside flag wrongly raised when he turned in Ribéry's low cross into the net with his torso a metre from the Ukrainian goal-line. Ukraine had won the first leg of the play-off 2–0 in <a href="/wiki/Kyiv" title="Kyiv">Kyiv</a> just four days earlier. France would eventually win the second leg 3–0 to advance to the 2014 World Cup finals in <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> with a 3–2 aggregate scoreline.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">&#91;275&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 June 2014, Benzema was named in France's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>, making his debut in the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-276" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-276">&#91;276&#93;</a></sup> In the team's first match, a 3–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Honduras_national_football_team" title="Honduras national football team">Honduras</a> in <a href="/wiki/Porto_Alegre" title="Porto Alegre">Porto Alegre</a> on 15 June, he scored a goal in each half, the first from a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty kick</a>. He also assisted the team's second goal when his shot rebounded off the post and was fumbled over the goal-line by Honduran goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Noel_Valladares" title="Noel Valladares">Noel Valladares</a> for an own goal, the first World Cup goal given by <a href="/wiki/Goal-line_technology" title="Goal-line technology">goal-line technology</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277">&#91;277&#93;</a></sup> He later added a third goal sealing France's 3–0 victory against Honduras. He was named by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> as man of the match for his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-278" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-278">&#91;278&#93;</a></sup> In the second group fixture, he scored and had a penalty saved in a 5–2 defeat of <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a>, as <i>Les Bleus</i> all but secured qualification to the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage" title="2014 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">knockout stage</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-279" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-279">&#91;279&#93;</a></sup> France were later knocked out by <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> in the quarter-final stage of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-280" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-280">&#91;280&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-281" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-281">&#91;281&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-282" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-282">&#91;282&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2016_and_2018_World_Cup">Euro 2016 and 2018 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Euro 2016 and 2018 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 13 April 2016, French Football Federation announced that Benzema would not be picked for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">Euro 2016</a> tournament on home soil.<sup id="cite_ref-Benzema_axed_from_France_283-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Benzema_axed_from_France-283">&#91;283&#93;</a></sup> He responded on 1 June 2016 in <i>Marca</i>, in an interview entitled 'Benzema: "Deschamps folded due to pressure from France's racist element"'.<sup id="cite_ref-284" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-284">&#91;284&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Benzema was also left off the roster for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-285" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-285">&#91;285&#93;</a></sup> Directing his frustration at FFF president <a href="/wiki/No%C3%ABl_Le_Gra%C3%ABt" title="Noël Le Graët">Noël Le Graët</a>, Benzema later tweeted: "Mr Le Graët, with all due respect, you've lost an opportunity to remain silent. I've discovered your true face, and this isn't the one that said he appreciated me and wouldn't discuss the subject of team selections!"<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286">&#91;286&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In November 2019, Benzema replied to Le Graët's comments that his career with France was over, by saying: "If you think I'm done, let me play with one of the other countries I am eligible for and we'll see".<sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287">&#91;287&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A creative, skillful, quick, agile, and prolific forward, who is good in the air and capable of playing off the shoulders of the last defender,<sup id="cite_ref-Karim_Benzema_to_Arsenal_288-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Karim_Benzema_to_Arsenal-288">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-289" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-289">&#91;289&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-290" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-290">&#91;290&#93;</a></sup> Benzema has been described as an "immensely talented <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a>" who is "strong and powerful" and "a potent finisher from inside the box" with either foot, as well as his head, despite being naturally right footed.<sup id="cite_ref-Bio_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bio-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Karim_Benzema_to_Arsenal_288-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Karim_Benzema_to_Arsenal-288">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup> An atypical <a href="/wiki/Squad_number_(association_football)" title="Squad number (association football)">number 9</a>, although he is usually deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Centre-forward" title="Forward (association football)">centre forward</a>, and can operate as an out-and-out striker, Benzema is also capable of playing in several other offensive positions, and has been used on the <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Winger" title="Forward (association football)">wing</a>, or even <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">behind the main striker</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Second_striker" title="Forward (association football)">number 10 or deep-lying forward</a>. In addition to his goalscoring, Benzema is known for his willingness and ability to drop into deeper or wider positions, and either link-up play with midfielders, or use his strength and technical ability to hold up the ball with his back to goal to provide <a href="/wiki/Assist_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Assist (football)">assists</a> for teammates, courtesy of his vision, creativity, passing, and eye for the final ball; because of his playing style, he has been described as a "nine and a half" in the media.<sup id="cite_ref-Karim_Benzema_to_Arsenal_288-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Karim_Benzema_to_Arsenal-288">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-291" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-291">&#91;291&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-return_292-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-return-292">&#91;292&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Karim_Benzema_is_the_perfect_striker_for_Real_293-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Karim_Benzema_is_the_perfect_striker_for_Real-293">&#91;293&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-294" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-294">&#91;294&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-295" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-295">&#91;295&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-296" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-296">&#91;296&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-297" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-297">&#91;297&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During his time at Real Madrid, Benzema has also been praised by pundits for his work-rate and tactical intelligence off the ball, as well as his positional sense and attacking movement as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a>, which often draws opposing defenders out of position, and in turn creates spaces for his teammates; as such, he formed a strong offensive partnership with <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> during the latter's time with the club. Indeed, Benzema's movement drew defenders away and created space for Ronaldo to make attacking runs into the centre of the area from the left wing, which essentially saw the Frenchman act as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#False_9" title="Forward (association football)">false 9</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-return_292-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-return-292">&#91;292&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Karim_Benzema_is_the_perfect_striker_for_Real_293-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Karim_Benzema_is_the_perfect_striker_for_Real-293">&#91;293&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-298" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-298">&#91;298&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-299" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-299">&#91;299&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-300" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-300">&#91;300&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-301" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-301">&#91;301&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r978413945/mw-parser-output/.tmulti">.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{display:flex;flex-direction:column}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .theader{clear:both;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;align-self:center;background-color:transparent;width:100%}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbcaption{background-color:transparent}.mw-parser-output (max-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{width:100%!important;box-sizing:border-box;max-width:none!important;align-items:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow{justify-content:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle{float:none!important;max-width:100%!important;box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle .thumbcaption{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow>.thumbcaption{text-align:center}}</style><div class="thumb tmulti tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:224px;max-width:224px"><div class="trow"><div class="tsingle" style="width:222px;max-width:222px"><div class="thumbimage"><a href="/wiki/File:Karim_Benzema_in_a_Real_Madrid_music_video.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" href="/wiki/File:Karim_Benzema_in_a_Real_Madrid_commercial.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Karim_Benzema_in_a_Real_Madrid_commercial.jpg/220px-Karim_Benzema_in_a_Real_Madrid_commercial.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Karim_Benzema_in_a_Real_Madrid_commercial.jpg/330px-Karim_Benzema_in_a_Real_Madrid_commercial.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Karim_Benzema_in_a_Real_Madrid_commercial.jpg/440px-Karim_Benzema_in_a_Real_Madrid_commercial.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1920" data-file-height="1080" /></a></div></div></div><div class="trow" style="display:flex"><div class="thumbcaption">Benzema in an <a href="/wiki/Adidas" title="Adidas">Adidas</a> music video (<i>above</i>) and a commercial (<i>below</i>) for Real Madrid in 2019 and 2018 respectively.</div></div></div></div>
<p>Karim Benzema was born in the city of <a href="/wiki/Lyon" title="Lyon">Lyon</a>, France to <a href="/wiki/Algerians_in_France" title="Algerians in France">French nationals of Algerian descent</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-302" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-302">&#91;302&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-303" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-303">&#91;303&#93;</a></sup> As a practicing <a href="/wiki/Muslim" class="mw-redirect" title="Muslim">Muslim</a>, he observes fasting during the Islamic holy month of <a href="/wiki/Ramadan" title="Ramadan">Ramadan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-goal_304-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal-304">&#91;304&#93;</a></sup> His grandfather, Da Lakehal Benzema, lived in the village of <a href="/wiki/Tigzirt" title="Tigzirt">Tigzirt</a>, located in the northern town of <a href="/wiki/Beni_Djellil" title="Beni Djellil">Beni Djellil</a> in <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a> before migrating to Lyon, where he eventually settled in the 1950s.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_background_305-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_background-305">&#91;305&#93;</a></sup> Benzema's father, Hafid, was born in Tigzirt, while his mother, Wahida Djebbara, was born and raised in Lyon; her family originated from <a href="/wiki/Oran" title="Oran">Oran</a>. Benzema is the third youngest in the family and grew up with eight other siblings in <a href="/wiki/Bron" title="Bron">Bron</a>, an eastern suburb of Lyon.<sup id="cite_ref-benzema_background_305-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-benzema_background-305">&#91;305&#93;</a></sup> His younger brothers Gressy and Sabri are also footballers.<sup id="cite_ref-306" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-306">&#91;306&#93;</a></sup> The former plays at the amateur level with Vaulx-le-Velin in the Division d'Honneur, the sixth division of French football, while the latter plays in the youth academy of a club in the family's hometown of Bron.<sup id="cite_ref-307" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-307">&#91;307&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-308" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-308">&#91;308&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 3 February 2014, his daughter Mélia was born.<sup id="cite_ref-309" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-309">&#91;309&#93;</a></sup> On 5 May 2017, his son Ibrahim was born.<sup id="cite_ref-310" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-310">&#91;310&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Since evolving internationally, Benzema has participated in numerous advertising campaigns.&#160;He was chosen as an ambassador of the American video game publisher&#160;<a href="/wiki/Electronic_Arts" title="Electronic Arts">Electronic Arts</a>&#160;for the&#160;FIFA&#160;series. He has signed several&#160;sponsorship&#160;contracts,&#160;notably with the Korean automobile manufacturer <a href="/wiki/Hyundai_Motor_Company" title="Hyundai Motor Company">Hyundai</a>, the French telephone operator&#160;<a href="/wiki/SFR" title="SFR">SFR</a> and its subsidiary&#160;BuzzMobile, the French bank&#160;<a href="/wiki/LCL_S.A." title="LCL S.A.">LCL</a>&#160;and the sports betting company&#160;<a href="/wiki/Bwin" title="Bwin">bwin</a>. Benzema is sponsored by&#160;<a href="/wiki/Adidas" title="Adidas">Adidas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-311" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-311">&#91;311&#93;</a></sup> In 2017, his documentary film <i>Le K Benzema</i> was released.<sup id="cite_ref-312" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-312">&#91;312&#93;</a></sup> In 2020, Benzema started his own <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a> channel, uploading videos of his everyday life, as well as interviews and fan <a href="/wiki/Interview" title="Interview">Q&amp;As</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-313" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-313">&#91;313&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-314" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-314">&#91;314&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Controversies_and_legal_issues">Controversies and legal issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Controversies and legal issues">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 6 December 2006, he told <a href="/wiki/Radio_Monte_Carlo" title="Radio Monte Carlo">RMC</a> about his possible selection for the <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algerian team</a>: "It's my parents' country, it's in my heart. But good after sporting, it's true that I will play in French team. I will be always present for the French team. Then it's more for the sporting side, because Algeria is my country, here, my parents come from there. After, France ... It's more sporty, that's it."<sup id="cite_ref-315" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-315">&#91;315&#93;</a></sup> Benzema drew some criticism for these comments, as well as for his reluctance to sing the French national anthem, "<a href="/wiki/La_Marseillaise" title="La Marseillaise">La Marseillaise</a>", before each match with the national team.<sup id="cite_ref-316" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-316">&#91;316&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-317" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-317">&#91;317&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 18 April 2010, it was first reported by French television channel <a href="/wiki/M6_(TV_channel)" title="M6 (TV channel)">M6</a> that four members of the French national team were being investigated for their roles as clients in a prostitute ring operated inside of a Paris nightclub, with some of the women possibly being underage. The players were eventually revealed to be Franck Ribéry, Sidney Govou, Hatem Ben Arfa and Benzema.<sup id="cite_ref-318" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-318">&#91;318&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-319" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-319">&#91;319&#93;</a></sup> Benzema was alleged to have had a sexual rendezvous with a prostitute when she was 16 years of age, an act Benzema denied through his lawyer.<sup id="cite_ref-320" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-320">&#91;320&#93;</a></sup> On 20 July, Benzema was questioned by Paris police and indicted on the charge of "solicitation of a minor prostitute".<sup id="cite_ref-321" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-321">&#91;321&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-322" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-322">&#91;322&#93;</a></sup> In November 2011, prosecutors asked for the cases against Ribéry and Benzema to be dropped, saying that the players were not aware that the escort, identified as <a href="/wiki/Zahia_Dehar" title="Zahia Dehar">Zahia Dehar</a>, was 16 years old.<sup id="cite_ref-323" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-323">&#91;323&#93;</a></sup> However, the case did go on to trial. In January 2014, the judge in the case dropped the charges against both Ribery and Benzema saying there was lack of sufficient evidence that the pair knew the prostitutes were underaged.<sup id="cite_ref-324" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-324">&#91;324&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 November 2015, Benzema was arrested by French police for his alleged part in <a href="/wiki/Blackmailing" class="mw-redirect" title="Blackmailing">blackmailing</a> fellow France international player <a href="/wiki/Mathieu_Valbuena" title="Mathieu Valbuena">Mathieu Valbuena</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-325" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-325">&#91;325&#93;</a></sup> During the investigation over the blackmail plot, French Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Valls" title="Manuel Valls">Manuel Valls</a> stated, "A great athlete should be exemplary. If he is not, he has no place in the France team. There are so many kids, so many youngsters in our suburbs that relate to great athletes. They wear the blue jersey, the colours of France, which are so important in these moments."<sup id="cite_ref-326" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-326">&#91;326&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-327" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-327">&#91;327&#93;</a></sup> On 10 December 2015, the president of the FFF <a href="/wiki/No%C3%ABl_Le_Gra%C3%ABt" title="Noël Le Graët">Noël Le Graët</a> announced the provisional suspension of the striker from <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">French team</a> until new development of the affair.<sup id="cite_ref-328" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-328">&#91;328&#93;</a></sup> On 17 February 2016, the judicial review was lifted by the investigating judge who allowed Karim Benzema to get in touch again with Mathieu Valbuena. On 11 July 2017, the <a href="/wiki/Court_of_Cassation_(France)" title="Court of Cassation (France)">Court of Cassation</a> issued a judgment in which it invalidated a decision of the Court of Appeal of Versailles, which had validated the procedure by which Benzema had been indicted for complicity of attempted blackmail. This decision was made on the basis of contesting the legality of the phone calls recording by the police, and the judgement did not disprove the veracity of the blackmail attempt on Valbuena by Benzema.<sup id="cite_ref-329" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-329">&#91;329&#93;</a></sup> On 7 January 2021, the public prosecutor's office in Versailles announced that Benzema would face trial for his alleged involvement in the blackmail attempt.<sup id="cite_ref-330" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-330">&#91;330&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In October 2020, controversy arose when it was discovered that Benzema, among a few other prominent French footballers liked a threatening <a href="/wiki/Instagram" title="Instagram">Instagram</a> post by ex-MMA fighter <a href="/wiki/Khabib_Nurmagomedov" title="Khabib Nurmagomedov">Khabib Nurmagomedov</a> calling for "the <a href="/wiki/God_in_Islam" title="God in Islam">Almighty</a> to disfigure the face of this creature", referring to <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a> <a href="/wiki/Emmanuel_Macron" title="Emmanuel Macron">Emmanuel Macron</a>. The post was written by Khabib in reaction to the French President publicly condemning the recent <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Samuel_Paty" title="Murder of Samuel Paty">murder of Samuel Paty</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-331" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-331">&#91;331&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honours">Honours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Karim_Benzema&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Honours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><b>Lyon</b><sup id="cite_ref-SW_343-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-343">&#91;336&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a>: <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_Ligue_1" title="2004–05 Ligue 1">2004–05</a>, <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_Ligue_1" title="2005–06 Ligue 1">2005–06</a>, <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_Ligue_1" title="2006–07 Ligue 1">2006–07</a>, <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Ligue_1" title="2007–08 Ligue 1">2007–08</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a>: <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Coupe_de_France" title="2007–08 Coupe de France">2007–08</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="Trophée des Champions">Trophée des Champions</a>: <a href="/wiki/2006_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2006 Trophée des Champions">2006</a>, <a href="/wiki/2007_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2007 Trophée des Champions">2007</a></li></ul>
<p><b>Real Madrid</b><sup id="cite_ref-SW_343-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-343">&#91;336&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a>: <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_La_Liga" title="2011–12 La Liga">2011–12</a>, <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_La_Liga" title="2016–17 La Liga">2016–17</a>, <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_La_Liga" title="2019–20 La Liga">2019–20</a><sup id="cite_ref-Liga_210-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liga-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup></li>
